(A) 24-well tissue culture plates were coated with anti-human IgG4 and anti-mouse IgG2a capture antibodies at 1 μg/ml in PBS, and incubated at 4°C, overnight. Appropriate stimuli added: Delta1-Fc or hIgG4 as control, both at 20 μg/ml in PBS and anti-CD3 (Hit3a, IgG2a) or mIgG as control, both at 1 μg/ml in PBS, and incubated at 37°C, 3 h. Plates were washed with PBS and positively selected hCD4+ T-cells were seeded at 2 × 106 cells/well, in 1 ml of media to a total of 1 × 107 cells/stimulation.">
